  <script>

// Javascript function to get cookie and read its value
function getCookie(cname) {
  var name = cname + "=";
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for(var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
      c = c.substring(1);
    }
    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
      return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
    }
  }
  return "";
}

      publir_show_ads = false;
    }

                <a id="main-content"></a>
                          <h1 class="title" id="page-title">Media Bias Ratings</h1>
                                          <div class="region region-help">
    <div id="block-block-95" class="block block-block first odd">
  
  	  
      	
  <style>
.landing p {  margin-top: 10px;  font-size: 18px;  line-height: 1.4; }
.landing h1, .landing h2, .landing h3, .landing h4, .landing h5, .landing h6 {  margin-top: 30px; }
.landing hr {  margin: 30px 0px;}

.gradient-border {  max-width: 1280;  position: relative;  margin: 1rem 0 1.5rem;  background: linear-gradient(124deg, rgba(182,19,27,1) 0%, rgba(128,79,144,1) 50%, rgba(36,78,146,1) 95%);  padding: 0 0 5px 5px; }
.gradient-border-inner {  background: #fff;  padding: .5rem;  line-height: 1.25 }
.gradient-border-inner h1, .gradient-border-inner h2, .gradient-border-inner h3, .gradient-border-inner h4, .gradient-border-inner h5, .gradient-border-inner h6 {  margin: 0 0 5px; }

.bg-jump-to-ratings {
    background-image:
    linear-gradient(to right, rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1) 0%, rgba(255, 255, 255, .8) 25%, rgba(255, 255, 255, 1) 70%),
    url('https://www.allsides.com/sites/default/files/jump-to-list-background.gif');
    background-position: left;
    background-repeat: no-repeat;
    margin: 10px 0;
    padding: 5px 0;
}

#jump-to-ratings { margin: 30px auto; }

    background-image:
    linear-gradient(to right, rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1) 0%, rgba(255, 255, 255, .8) 15%, rgba(255, 255, 255, 1) 70%),
    url('https://www.allsides.com/sites/default/files/jump-to-list-background.gif');
}
}

@media (max-width: 767px) {

    background-image:
    linear-gradient(to top, rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.4), rgba(255, 255, 255, 1)),
    url('https://www.allsides.com/sites/default/files/jump-to-list-background.gif');

#support.bg-color-gradient { background: linear-gradient(to left, #258156, white); }

<section class="landing">

<p><span style="font-size:24px;"><strong>Everyone is biased.</strong></span> AllSides Media Bias Ratings<sup>™</sup> help you to easily identify different perspectives so you can get the full picture and think for yourself.</p>

<div class="banner-outer bg-jump-to-ratings" id="jump-to-ratings">
<div class="banner-inner">
<div class="row-fluid">
      <div class="span6 offset2">
<p><strong>Top outlets appear in our chart, but we've rated over 800 sources.</strong></p>
      </div>
      <div class="span4" style="text-align:center;">
<a href="#ratings"><div class="btn btn-success btn-full-width">Jump to list of ratings</div></a>
      </div>

</div>
</div>
</div>

<p>Hidden bias misleads and divides us. By making the political leanings of hundreds of media sources transparent, AllSides frees people from one-sided <a href="https://www.allsides.com/filter-bubbles" target="_blank">filter bubbles</a> so they can better understand the world — and each other.</p>

<p>Knowing the political bias of media outlets allows you to <a href="https://www.allsides.com/unbiased-balanced-news" target="_blank">consume a balanced news diet</a> and avoid manipulation and fake news.</p>

<div style="text-align:center; max-width:500px;margin:auto auto;">
<a href="/media-bias/media-bias-chart"><img style="border: 1px solid #353C40; margin-bottom:10px;" src="https://www.allsides.com/sites/default/files/AllSidesMediaBiasChart-Version3.jpg"  /></a>
<div style="text-align: center;" class="sharethis-inline-share-buttons"></div>
</div>

<p>We provide separate bias ratings for news and editorial/opinion content for a number of outlets. <strong>Unless otherwise noted, all bias ratings are based on online, written content, <em>not</em> broadcast, TV, or radio content.</strong> Our ratings are fluid and subject to change over time as new information is gathered and biases change. To see the ratings in action, visit <a href="https://www.allsides.com/unbiased-balanced-news" target="_blank">our balanced newsfeed</a>.</p>

<hr style="max-width:500px; margin: 30px auto;">

<!--METHODOLOGY-->
<h3 style="font-weight:normal;text-align:center;"><a class="black-link" href="/media-bias/media-bias-rating-methods">How AllSides Rates Media Bias</a></h3>
<p><strong>AllSides uses <a href="/media-bias/media-bias-rating-methods">multipartisan, scientific analysis to rate bias</a>.</strong> Our methodology is scientific, but each individual will have a subjective opinion of the bias of any given outlet. We reflect the average view of Americans, not one individual.</p>
   <p>We use  <a href="/media-bias/media-bias-rating-methods">multiple methods to rate media bias</a>, including editorial reviews, blind bias surveys, independent reviews, and third party research.</p>

<hr style="max-width:500px; margin: 30px auto;">

<!--WHAT THE RATINGS MEAN-->
<h3 style="font-weight:normal;text-align:center;">What the Ratings Mean</h3>
<div class="row-fluid">
<div class="span8">
   <p>Learn what it means for an outlet to be <a href="http://www.allsides.com/bias/left" target="_blank">Left</a>, <a href="https://www.allsides.com/media-bias/left-center" target="_blank">Lean Left</a>, <a href="http://www.allsides.com/bias/center" target="_blank">Center</a>, <a href="http://www.allsides.com/bias/right-center" target="_blank">Lean Right</a>, <a href="http://www.allsides.com/bias/right" target="_blank">Right</a>, or <a href="https://www.allsides.com/media-bias/allsides" target="_blank">Mixed</a>.</p>
<p><strong>Center doesn't mean better! </strong> A Center outlet may still omit important perspectives, or run individual articles that display bias, while not displaying a lot of predictable bias frequently. <a href="https://www.allsides.com/unbiased-balanced-news" target="_blank">Read news across the spectrum to get the full picture</a>.</p>

</div>


<div class="span4">
<div style="max-width: 350px;margin: auto;">
<img src="/sites/all/themes/allsides/images/bias-all.png" />
<a href="/rate-own-bias" class="btn btn-large btn-block btn-primary"><strong>Discover your bias</strong><br><small>Rate your own bias and see how you compare to others.</small></a>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</section>
</div><!-- /.block -->

<h4>Which candidate did you favor in the 2020 presidential election?</h4>

<a class="btn btn-large btn-success" id="starting-question-1-president-trump" href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSc86_LJw5BEa_9BrSxkWZVHCWMYTybYxftqZxA6A_cdm2Ydpg/viewform?usp=pp_url&entry.976214662=Trump" >Trump</a>

<div id="block-block-175" class="block block-block last odd">
  
  	  
      	
  <a id="ratings"></a>
<hr style="max-width:500px; margin: 30px auto;">

<h3>AllSides Media Bias Ratings<sup>™</sup></h3>

<div class="row-fluid">
<div class="span8">

<p><strong>Submit a source.</strong> Before contacting us, please browse <a href="https://www.allsides.com/media-bias/media-bias-ratings?field_featured_bias_rating_value=All#ratings">all of our ratings</a> to ensure we haven’t already rated the source. Still don’t see it? <a href="mailto:feedback@allsides.com?subject=Missing Source Suggestion&amp;body=Please add the following source(s):" target="_blank">Email us.</a></p>

<p><strong>Improve our ratings.</strong> Click <strong>agree</strong> or <strong>disagree</strong> below to give feedback. Community votes don't determine our ratings, but act as valuable feedback that a rating may need review.</p>
</div>

          </td>
